+  id            String      @id@default(cuid()) 
+  odontogram    Odontogram  @relation(fields: [odontogram_id], references: [id])   
+  odontogram_id String 
+    abscent          Boolean
+  notes            String?
+  //Periogram
+  mesial_vestibular_depth Float?
+  mesial_vestibular_gmh Float?
+  mesial_vestibular_lci Float?
+  mesial_vestibular_probing_bleeding Boolean?
+
+  medial_vestibular_depth Float?
+  medial_vestibular_gmh Float?
+  medial_vestibular_lci Float?
+  medial_vestibular_probing_bleeding Boolean?
+
+  distal_vestibular_depth Float?
+  distal_vestibular_gmh Float?
+  distal_vestibular_lci Float?
+  distal_vestibular_probing_bleeding Boolean?
+
+  mesial_lingual_depth            Float?
+  mesial_lingual_gmh              Float?
+  mesial_lingual_lci              Float?
+  mesial_lingual_probing_bleeding Boolean?
+
+  medial_lingual_depth            Float?
+  medial_lingual_gmh              Float?
+  medial_lingual_lci              Float?
+  medial_lingual_probing_bleeding Boolean?
+
+  distal_lingual_depth            Float?
+  distal_lingual_gmh              Float?
+  distal_lingual_lci              Float?
+  distal_lingual_probing_bleeding Boolean?
+  mobility                        Boolean?
+  if_yes_mobility_level           String?
+  periogram_date                  DateTime?
+  // Tooth 
+  higid                      Boolean?
+  vestibular_biofilm         Boolean?
+  palatin_biofilm            Boolean?
+  oclusal_biofilm            Boolean?
+  mesial_biofilm             Boolean?
+  distal_biofilm             Boolean?
+  poor_restoration           Boolean?
+  if_yes_what_type_of_restoration Restorations_types?
+  caries_white_spot_lesion   Boolean?
+  if_yes_where_white_lesion  String?
+  active_carie               Boolean?
+  inative_carie              Boolean?
+  cavity_caries_lesion       Boolean?
+  if_yes_where_cavity_lesion String?
+  if_yes_depth               Float?
+  extense_carie_lesion       Boolean?
+  fluorosis_white_lesions    Boolean?
+  if_yes_fuorosis_level      String?
+  black_hash                 Boolean?
+  enamel_fissure             Boolean?
+  dentin_fissure             Boolean?
+  if_yes_fissure_direction   String?
+  enamel_fracture            Boolean?
+  if_yes_fracture_size       String?
+  dental_erosion             Boolean?
+  dental_abfraction          Boolean?
+  dental_atriction           Boolean?
+  dental_abrasion            Boolean?
+  dental_anomaly             Boolean?
+  if_yes_anomaly_description String?
+  // Endodontics
+  initial_radiograph         Boolean?
+  final_radiograph           Boolean?
+  pulp_status                Pulp_states?
+  canal_calcifications       Boolean?
+    atresic_pulp_chamber       Boolean?     
+  canal_depth_probing        Boolean?
+       
+  canal_depth_in_mm          Float?
+
+  number_of_roots            Int? @default(1)
+  number_of_canals           Int? 
+  acessory_canal             Boolean?
+  lateral_canal              Boolean?
+  //Cirurgy
+  hiper_cementosis           Boolean?
+  bone_petrosis              Boolean?
+  root_dilacerations         Boolean?
+  cirurgy_indication         Boolean?
+  reason_of_indication       String?
+  simple_removal             Boolean?
+  difficult_removal          Boolean?
+  antibiotcs_prevention_needed Boolean?
+  // What changed
+  createdAt DateTime @default(now())
+  updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt
+  what_was_updated String[]

+  anamnesis_prontuary Anamnesis @relation(fields: [anamnesis_prontuary_id], references: [id])
+  anamnesis_prontuary_id String
+  // Health Information
+  main_issue String
+  recent_disease_history String
+  undergoing_medical_treatment yes_no
+  if_yes_what_treatment String?
+  taking_any_medication yes_no
+  if_yes_what_medication String?
+  // Allergies
+  already_used_local_anestesics yes_no
+  you_presented_reaction yes_no 
+  allergic_to_any_medicine yes_no
+  if_yes_what_medicine String?
+  allergic_to_latex yes_no
+  //Hemodinamics
+  has_any_know_blood_issues yes_no
+  use_acetil_salicilic_acid yes_no
+  if_yes_for_what String?
+  you_have_already_made_blood_testing yes_no
+  if_yes_when_made_it DateTime?
+  has_any_importanting_bleeding yes_no
+  if_yes_when DateTime?
+  if_yes_how_long_to_stop String
+  have_problems_with_healing yes_no
+  // Hormonal disease
+  has_any_know_tireoids_issues yes_no
+  has_any_know_hormonal_issues yes_no
+  you_are_using_any_corticosteroids yes_no
+  diabetes_mellitus yes_no
+  if_yes_any_treatment_for_diabetes String?
+  // Health of hearth
+  any_heart_problems yes_no
+  if_yes_what_hearth_problem String?
+  arterial_hypertension yes_no
+  if_yes_any_treatment_for_hypertension String?
+  // Lungs health
+  breathing_problems yes_no
+  if_yes_what_breathing_problem String?
+  // Kidneys health
+  kidney_damage yes_no
+  if_yes_what_kidney_problem String?
+  // Gastric Health
+  gastric_problems yes_no
+  if_yes_you_looked_for_gastric_doctor yes_no?
+  if_yes_what_gastric_problems String?
+  // General health information
+  have_rheumatic_fever yes_no
+  joints_problems_or_reumatics yes_no
+  if_yes_you_looked_for_reaumatics_doctor String?
+  use_drugs yes_no
+  if_yes_what_drug String?
+  smoker yes_no
+  if_yes_how_many_cigarretes_perday Int?
+  consider_a_alcolic_addicted yes_no
+  if_yes_when_was_the_last_drink String?
+  family_background yes_no
+  if_yes_what_familys_problems String?
+  //Woman
+  preagnant yes_no
+  if_yes_how_many_months String?

+  what_contraceptives String?
+  are_breastfeeding yes_no

+  if_yes_guided_by_the_gynecologist yes_no?
+  take_hormone yes_no
+  take_calcium yes_no
+  // Information
+  terms_readed yes_no
+  patient_signed yes_no
+  signed_date DateTime
+  createdAt DateTime @default(now())
+  updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt
+  what_was_updated String[] 
+}

+model Dont_know_questions {
+  id               String       @unique @default(cuid())
+  question         String
+  questionnaire_id String
+}
+
+model Dentist {
+  id            String       @id@default(uuid())
+  CRO_number    String       @unique
+  firstname     String
+  lastname      String
+  username      String       @default(cuid()) 
+  password      String       @default(cuid())
+  contactmeans  Contact_means?
+  shedule       Schedule     
+  cellphone_number String?
+  clinic    Clinic   @relation("Clinic_relation", fields: [clinic_id], references: [registered_id])
+  clinic_id String
+  email     Email[]
+  active    Boolean  @default(true)
+  specialization Clinic_specializations[]
+  ortodontics_treatments Ortodontics[]
+  implantology_treatments Implantology[]  
+  comission Float?
+  patients  Patient[]   @relation(references: [id])
+  createdAt DateTime @default(now())
+  updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt
+  role      String   @default("DENTIST")
+
+}
+
+model Clinic_specializations {
+   id         Int         @id @default(autoincrement())
+   specialization Specializations
+   createdAt DateTime @default(now())
+   updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt
+}
+
+enum Specializations {
+   ORAL_MAXILLOFACIAL_SURGERY_AND_TRAUMATOLOGY
+   DENTISTRY
+   TEMPORO_MANDIBULAR_AND_OROFACIAL_PAIN_DYSFUNCTION
+   ENDODONTICS
+   IMPLANTOLOGY
+   PEDIATRIC_DENTISTRY
+   ORTHODONTICS
+   PERIODONTICS 
+   RADIOLOGY
+   COLLECTIVE_HEALTH
+   STOMATOLOGY
+   ELDERLY_DENTIST
+   FORENSIC_DENTISTRY
+   PATIENTS_WITH_SPECIAL_NEEDS
+   OCCUPATIONAL_DENTISTRY
+   DENTAL_PROSTHESIS
+   ORAL_AND_MAXILLOFACIAL_PROSTHESIS
+   ORAL_PATHOLOGY
+}
+
+model Employeer {
+  id        String      @id @default(uuid())
+  firstname String
+  lastname  String
+  username  String  @default(cuid()) 
+  password  String   @default(cuid())
+  clinic    Clinic   @relation(fields: [clinic_id], references: [registered_id])
+  clinic_id String
+  role      Clinic_Roles  @relation(fields: [role_id], references: [id])
+  role_id   String
+  createdAt DateTime @default(now())
+  updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt
+}
+
+model Clinic_Roles {
+  id           String      @id @default(cuid())
+  name         String
+  description  String?
+  employer     Employeer[]
+  createdAt    DateTime @default(now())
+  updatedAt    DateTime @updatedAt
+}
+
+model Dental_insurance {
+  id        String     @id @default(cuid())
+  name      String   @unique
+  clinic    Clinic[]   @relation(references: [registered_id])
+  compensation_date  Int?
+  compensation_value Int?
+  procedures_values  Clinic_procedures_insurance_values
+  active    Boolean  @default(true)
+  createdAt DateTime @default(now())
+  updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt
+}
+
+enum Contact_means {
+  WHATTSAPP_message
+  WHATTSAPP_call
+  CALL
+  SMS
+}
+
+enum Phonetypes {
+  BRASILIAN_CELLPHONE_NUMBER
+  BRASILIAN_FIX_NUMBER
+  EUA_NUMBER
+  NONE
+}
+
+enum Language {
+  ENGLISH
+  PORTUGUESE
+}
